# <a name="azure-resource-manager-resource-provider-operations"></a><span data-ttu-id="a3472-103">Azure Resource Manager 資源提供者作業</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a3472-103">Azure Resource Manager Resource Provider operations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a3472-104">本文件會列出每個 Microsoft Azure Resource Manager 資源提供者可用的作業。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a3472-104">This document lists the operations available for each Microsoft Azure Resource Manager resource provider.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a3472-105">這些作業可用在自訂角色中，以對 Azure 中的資源提供細微的角色型存取控制 (RBAC) 權限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a3472-105">These can be used in custom roles to provide granular Role-Based Access Control (RBAC) permissions to resources in Azure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a3472-106">請注意，這份清單並不完整，而且這些作業可能會隨著每個提供者的更新而有所新增或移除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a3472-106">Please note this is not a comprehensive list and operations may be added or removed as each provider is updated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a3472-107">作業字串遵循 `Microsoft.<ProviderName>/<ChildResourceType>/<action>` 的格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a3472-107">Operation strings follow the format of `Microsoft.<ProviderName>/<ChildResourceType>/<action>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a3472-108">如需完整的現行清單，請使用 `Get-AzureRmProviderOperation` (在 PowerShell 中) 或 `azure provider operations show` (在 Azure CLI 中) 來列出 Azure 資源提供者的作業。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a3472-108">For a comprehensive and current list please use `Get-AzureRmProviderOperation` (in PowerShell) or `azure provider operations show` (in Azure CLI) to list operations of Azure resource providers.</span></span>
